<Time>1588627317911< /Time><rating>1</rating>< Text>
I frequent this convenience store, because it is the closest store that sells snacks, beer, drinks, etc. However, service quality has recently plummeted. I stopped by and bought a scratch-off lottery ticket, and I happen to win. Being excited about a semi-decent win for $100( on a $20 ticket), I returned to cash in the ticket the next day. I was turned away because they said they didn't have enough cash in the register. I understood the first day, and returned again the second day to find the same thing. Finally, the third day I bring the ticket in and even make a sizeable purchase for nearly $50, when I didn't plan on making a purchase at all. But, I figured it would help bring down the "cash back" amount. The middle-aged woman, who could hardly speak proper English proceeds to get upset because I was trying to cash the very lottery ticket I bought from that location. I explain that if you cannot cash out scratch-off lottery tickets, then you shouldn't sell them. She proceeds to get angry and tells me I have to pay for everything out of pocket. I told her the only reason I got this much to begin with was to help lower the funds she needed to return to me. Reluctantly, she throws a fit and clicked a few buttons on the cash register, which made the safe dispense the cash needed. SO, YOU MEAN TO TELL ME FOR THE LAST 3 DAYS, ALL YOU HAD TO DO WAS PRESS THREE BUTTONS! There is no excuse. THIS IS LAZINESS. Yes, there are a couple employees here that I have great respect for and they are extremely helpful. This was a horrible experience though, especially when I came back three separate times...</Text>

< review>
Wow, between the beautiful view, the wonderful and attentive service, and the delicious food, I'm thoroughly impressed with Chinatown restaurant. The man who I assume is the owner was so kind and even brought me an apple for good luck as I was leaving and thanked me for coming in and giving him some work to do.

In Chinatown, it can be difficult to choose a place to eat, you would be making a great decision to eat here. I tried to tip 40% but the owner gave me back some change and said he would just prefer I come back to eat here again, which i will be doing tomorrow because it is that good.<//review>

<text>Overall location gets a 4.5. There is quite a bit here, but not exactly a lot either. Asada burrito and tacos are great! Red and green sauce are excellent and unique. Little bit of heat on both. Food was awesome, will come back again soon to try more. This location is a small grocery also. They don't have a huge selection, but you could make just about any mexican food item you want with what can be found inside. Was quite pleased to find marjoram on the spice wall and a few other items you don't find everywhere. Serve Thrifty ice cream, decent looking meat counter. The pan dulce selection was really limited, had hoped for more. Staff were extremely friendly, was warmly greeted and assisted. Neighborhood location is in, not that great, will want to be aware of your surroundings when you are there. Location is clean, but could stand for some upgrades. Decent amount of parking, should be really easy to get to, very close to freeway. Parking, entrance and aisles are all accessible. Visit during COVID, so no chairs and didn't see a bathroom. Will return again soon, possibly best burritos for 5 miles around. Beans and rice great for burritos, but not best rice and beans ever had.

Pretty good food! You get chips and salsa at the table. yummy. 3 kinds of salsa. Ocean views! Pretty much anywhere you sit, you can see the ocean.

I got a chicken torta. So good! There wasn't very much meat. But it was still really good. Great flavors. Does not come with any side.

Hubby got 2 Al Pastor soft tacos. Sour cream on the side. Came with onion and guac. They were delicious! Very tiny though.  Came with beans and rice. Both basic. Nothing special.

No drinks. Just water. Came to around 27 bucks. Not bad. The portions are on the small side though.

The service was OK. Attentive, but not friendly. They all had very serious faces. No smiles. No small talk. A bit cold. But, this seems to be normal these days.

Food was pretty good. Great views. They also have a bar inside, and the bathroom is outside. Parking is limited. Small lot. There we're about 12 cars in the lot, with a few spare. But only 4 tables occupied. We will be back.

We had a night off, and decided to drive down here to have dinner. It's off on a side street. No ocean view. It's in a tiny shopping center, that almost looks deserted. Super easy to find, since there is a large sign on Hwy 1.

Just a couple of people inside when we arrived. Pretty quiet. The girl who helped us was friendly. Must be family operated, there was a toddler running arround.

We ordered the carnitas fries to share. They were very good. Had pork, cheese, and sour cream. We got pico de gallo on the side, since  hubby can't eat it. He got a beer, and I got a pineapple soda.

I ordered 2 hard tacos. One chicken, and one carne asada. Both were good. But 3 bites. I didn't get any sides. Hubby got 3 soft tacos. Those were 2 bites. Tacos are good, but VERY small. He got beans and rice. Both were good. I LOVED the rice. Very moist and flavorful.

You also get chips for the table. They have 3 salsas. But they are all runny, and just liquid. We didn't care for any of them. Food was decent, but not amazing.</review>< name>

I remembered this location as having been a roadhouse from a previous coast trip several years back.  This time it was Antonio's, and I'm glad we tried it!  We were in town for 4 days.  We tried Antonio's for dinner the first night and everything, in our opinion, was perfect!  We ended up eating lunch or dinner there 2 more times.
